*********************************************************************************
Commit: d1af998f1d77a2b105d9b7e80630b79965dac9af 
*********************************************************************************


  After Warm or Cold restart BLE Keyboard is removed in UEFI mode
  
  [Issue Description]
  In case of a specific Keyboard, after G3 or Warm or Cold restart BLE-Keyboard is removed in UEFI mode. Its a device specific issue, After connecting the KB and going for a warm or cold reboot, the device is expected to be auto connected, but the device is been removed in UEFI.
  
  [Resolution]
  That specific KB IDAddr is getting invalid during bonding, so fallback to Direct_BD_ADDR Or BDAddr which is valid at that time.
  
  Package/Module: Intel\Features\BluetoothPkg\BluetoothBusDxe
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  WCL/PTL
  ^^^ ^^^ 
  
  Hsd-es-id: 16028646296
  Change-Id: I731240b05986f104b92e9d9ab773de40fadd83c9
  Original commit hash: 4e614e24822749a69a7a36a3e86c7b3a04938db2
  
  [Changed Files]

*********************************************************************************


  SndwAccess: Next codec getter deadloop fix
  
  [Issue Description]

  is assumed to have unique ID. It is possible to have multiple

      ^^^

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 239c255e3a0cc8ebf8c2598c49e4e45b680201d2 
*********************************************************************************


  Remove "Disable NPK pre-BIOS tracing (Undo trace)" programming
  
  [Feature Description]
  Below settings can be removed from BIOS and PMC FW. Previously we added
  the steps to the PTI leakage issue. The issue should be fixed in silicon so
      ^^^^                                                        ^^^^^^^^^   
  steps can be removed.
  ^^^^                  
  
  Write all "0's" to NPK.NDB_CTRL.NDB_WAITEMPTY.
  - De-assert NPK.SCR.STOREENOVRD4 (stop STH trace storage).
  - De-assert NPK.SCR.STOREENOVRD5 (stop DTF trace storage).
  - Wait for pipeline empty by reading this status register, NPK.GTHSTAT.IBE4.
  - Wait for pipeline empty by reading this status register, NPK.GTHSTAT.IBE5.
  
  Package/Module: OneSiliconPkg/IpBlock/TraceHub
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  ALL
  
  Hsd-es-id: 15018284604
  Change-Id: I72b677e4408e8aa3fac6a1e9f7fd22c03a262405
  Original commit hash: 226bf6a1df8fee2a11fd2240c24a28add5acb5ae

[PCH]

  [PTL] Enable LONTIUM from New PCD instead of Embedded PCD.
   ^^^                                                       
  
  [Issue Description]
  This commit enables LONTIUM camera from a new PCD instead of
  Embedded PCD. This is done to avoid the dependency on Embedded PCD
  for LONTIUM camera. The new PCD is defined in MipiCamFeaturePkg.
  
  [Resolution]

  camera. The PCD is used in MipiCamInstallTableDxe to enable the
  LONTIUM camera. The Embedded PCD is no longer required for LONTIUM
  camera.
